  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_f12bf49f-2767-4726-9a7c-cb4f2894a7a3'
      });

  <span id="freeText2801273376924342822" style="display:none">"He was my darkness and I was his light. We couldn't exist without each other."<br /><br />For me, life was simple. I went to school and studied. I spent time with my friends and stayed out of trouble. I didn't drink or swear and I only dated gentlemen. I was the typical good girl with a bright future. My world seemed perfect. <br /><br />But that was about to change.<br /><br />Ryder Delaney was the one imperfection in my life. He was the bad boy, the black sheep, the one your mother always warned you about. He had only one hard-and-fast rule - Don't fall in love. <br /><br />But some rules were meant to be broken.<br /><br />We were best friends, inseparable since childhood despite our differences. I knew the real man hiding behind the tattoos and bad attitude. He knew all my secrets and dreams. But he didn't know there was one thing I wanted and couldn't have...him.<br /><br />But sometimes Fate has a way of intervening. Soon our world collapsed. War erupted. Darkness prevailed. Alone and on the run, our only goal was to survive and to ignore the feelings we had for each other. But love is powerful...<br /><br />and so is the darkness.<br /><br /><b>word count: 100,285 </b></span>

          $$('div.prototip').each(function(i){i.setStyle({zIndex: $('box').getStyle('z-index')})});
        } else {
          $$('div.prototip').each(function(i){i.setStyle({zIndex: 6000})});
        }
      });
      $('rating_details_tip').observe('prototip:hidden', function () {
        $$('span.elementTwo').each(function (e) {
          if (e.getStyle('display') !== 'none') {
            var lessLink = e.next();
            swapContent(lessLink);
          }
        });
      });

</script>  </div>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/587658614" />
    <a title="Jennifer Kyle" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/9916227-jennifer-kyle"><img alt="Jennifer Kyle" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1514915429p2/9916227.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/587658614?book_show_action=true">Apr 11, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jennifer Kyle" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jennifer Kyle" href="/user/show/9916227-jennifer-kyle">Jennifer Kyle</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/17788470-promise-me-darkness">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9916227-jennifer-kyle?shelf=para-dystopian-sci-fi-fantasy">para-dystopian-sci-fi-fantasy</a>

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer587658614" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5918510581266734084"><b>Nope Nope Nope</b> <br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/500725.gif' width='302' height='220' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Maddie is a nursing student and Ryder is the local manwhore/bad ass. They have been best friends for fifteen years. When they run into each other at a local bar during a hometown visit she finds out Ryder has decided to enlist in the military and wants to spend his last couple days staying with Maddie at her apartment by her school.<br/><br/>Things are pretty normal, well not really it seems that The United States of America is on the verge of war against terrorist countries. Maddie is dati</span>
  <span id="freeText5918510581266734084" style="display:none"><b>Nope Nope Nope</b> <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/500725.gif" width="302" height="220" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Maddie is a nursing student and Ryder is the local manwhore/bad ass. They have been best friends for fifteen years. When they run into each other at a local bar during a hometown visit she finds out Ryder has decided to enlist in the military and wants to spend his last couple days staying with Maddie at her apartment by her school.<br><br>Things are pretty normal, well not really it seems that The United States of America is on the verge of war against terrorist countries. Maddie is dating a guy name Ben and is a virgin. <br><br>Ryder is total alpha about her and saves her from a horrific event. Ryder puts the moves on her which confuses her because she doesn’t want to be another conquest for him but she too has feelings other than friendship. Truthfully, these two being friends for fifteen years doesn’t work for me they have no inside jokes, fun stories or anything!<br><br>Okay so back to this story, Maddie gives her “v”card to Ryder and here’s what he says before:<br><br><b>
  <i>”Years, Maddie,” he said, huskily. “I’ve wanted you for years.”</i>
</b><br><br>And here’s what he says after:<br><br><b>
  <i>”Shit, Maddie. What do you want me to do? Marry you? Put a ring on your finger? It was only sex.”</i>
</b><br><br><b>
  <i>”We’re just friends, Maddie. That won’t change. But I told you before, I don’t do relationships and I don’t have girlfriends.”</i>
</b><br><br>Okay so Ryder throws some crazy mixed signals but a reader can pretty much tell where the author is going with this romance. Ryder loves her but keeps pushing her away, been there done that as reader. <br> <br>They are at a club the earth starts shaking and the whole country losses power and society has fallen apart. Ryder, Maddie, Eva and Brody head back to their family’s homes. <br> <br>All the while Maddie is not worried about the state of our union but about her and Ryder’s relationship. <b>GIVE ME A BREAK</b>. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/409890.gif" width="299" height="220" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>They are attacked, without transportation, hurt and on the verge of dehydration and this chick is worried about her love life????<br><br>The foursome finds their way back home. Maddie’s father is in bad shape their town has crumbled but Maddie is still stuck on her “maybe” relationship. <br> <br>Then the ending…<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380400348ra/775634.gif" width="299" height="220" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I’m sorry, I’m out, I wish this cast of characters best of luck in the next book. Sadly, I’m not interested in the least on what will happen next. <br><br><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="5918510581266734084" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/591821660" />
    <a title="Lauren" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2629054-lauren"><img alt="Lauren" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1362350909p2/2629054.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/591821660?book_show_action=true">Apr 16, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer591821660" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16222344018426994575">**May contain spoilers**<br/><br/>Awful. Completely terrible. Months later it still makes me angry to think about. <br/><br/>...The plot was actually somewhat unique (although, Revolution anyone?). The descriptions of the whole electromagnetic pulse thing was good enough for me (not a physics/engineering/whatever-subject-that-is person). And then the nursing care stuff was relatively accurate (RN here), besides Maddie being an awful patient - (yay lets punch someone with my broken hand) but hey not all nurses are t</span>
  <span id="freeText16222344018426994575" style="display:none">**May contain spoilers**<br><br>Awful. Completely terrible. Months later it still makes me angry to think about. <br><br>...The plot was actually somewhat unique (although, Revolution anyone?). The descriptions of the whole electromagnetic pulse thing was good enough for me (not a physics/engineering/whatever-subject-that-is person). And then the nursing care stuff was relatively accurate (RN here), besides Maddie being an awful patient - (yay lets punch someone with my broken hand) but hey not all nurses are the best patients so - benefit of the doubt. <br><br>HOWEVER<br><br>I did not like this. And I really just hated the characters beyond words.<br><br><b>How I feel about Maddie:</b><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380412412ra/810913.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I really just couldn't get over how she kept putting herself and everyone in danger time and time again. She never had any character growth. She was stubborn to a fault. She was whiny. She had absolutely NO common sense. I just can't stand a character like that. Also she was the typical cliched "21-year-old virgin" who was waiting for true love but then gave it up to her player best friend who treated her like a floozy as she knew he would. And her personality was weird. She was this quiet innocent thing one section and then she'd be like punching Ryder and acting stubborn about the dumbest things... <br><br>I'd just like to point out a few scenes. <br><br>I think it really started to hit home for me how much I hated her when she started complaining about breaking into an empty house. Um okay Maddie. Let's stop and reflect. You have no food, no water, no shelter, got robbed of your car and almost all your supplies, the house is empty, no electricity works, no cars work, there's pretty much no chance of the house owners being able to get back to their house, and you're most likely going to die if you just hang out or keep walking. But let's just keep walking because breaking into the house would be <b>so wrong</b>. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/496481.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>It's a violent world out there now - she witnessed it firsthand - UGH STOP BEING DUMB AND JUST GO INTO THE DAMN HOUSE. <br><br>Then we have when they have gotten back to Ryder's home and the guys hear that there is trouble in town and decide to go check it out. Maddie hears that they are going and decides that she has to go too. Um okay Maddie. Let's set the scene here. TROUBLE in town. VIOLENCE. WAR. And then Maddie. Who has a broken rib, broken fingers, is described as tiny and little, gets basically knocked down by the wind, and has proven multiple times that she causes danger to herself and everyone around her. Also she likes to ignore the warning signs even when she sees them. YEAH Maddie you can go with them into town, okay. NOT. And then when they tell her no, she throws a temper tantrum and decides that fine if she can't go with them she's going to go to her house instead, with her dad who is dying of a stroke (great protection system there). <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/655929.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I think I am starting to understand why Ryder is so violent. Because this girl is an idiot and DOES NOT LISTEN. Ryder's mom says no, she knows Ryder and the others will be mad, but oh well they have to go anyway. <br><br>And then we have the next scene. At the house, when the convicts show up. There was a fleeting moment where I thought, oh my, is she actually going to prove herself?!?! She thinks - I hear someone, oh no! ... OH WAIT! I'VE GOT A GUN TO PROTECT US!! And then......... nothing. Let me just stand here immobile while the bad guy comes up and grabs me, takes away my gun, and heads off into the bedroom to rape me. Hm. Okay then. I almost started to warm up to her. But no. I did however slightly enjoy the next scene when she slices him in the brachial artery and he bleeds out. Nursing props I suppose. I guess if she has no common sense at least she has an education. <br><br>Alrighty so later on she goes and gets herself pregnant (love how there was like no concern on the character's part about the fact they're now living in a world without medical care and whatnot). And then she and Ryder are fighting and she's acting like a 3 year old. "I'm not hungry, I'm not going to eat because you want me to eat!! WAHH!!" Um HI dummy. Okay listen. I get that you have some weird stubborn pride thing or something BS but um YOU'RE PREGNANT NOW. That means you feed a baby when you eat. That means STFU and stop being an idiot and trying to kill the child that already has a decreased risk of surviving in this wacky world as it is. OK? Nope not okay. Still have seen no character development out of her. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1385851187ra/7242302.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I fear for this child. <br><br>Okay so just one more scene on Maddie, because I haven't even touched Ryder yet. End of the book - knock on the door... DANGER DANGER, PEOPLE HOLDING HER BACK. Someone calls her name, there's a GUN at the door. She hears her name and JUMPS UP AND RUNS TOWARDS IT while everyone around her tries to hold her back. Stubborn and dumbly she ends up staring down the barrel of a gun. MADDIE YOU IDIOT. YOU ARE PREGNANT NOW. THAT MEANS YOU NEED TO STOP DOING STUPID THINGS AND LISTEN TO THE OTHER MUCH SMARTER PEOPLE AROUND YOU THAT ACTUALLY HAVE A SURVIVAL INSTINCT AND COMMON SENSE. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1385851701ra/7242359.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1385851701ra/7242360.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>UGH. I am SO done with her. I am getting angry again just talking about it. On to Ryder...<br><br>---<br><br>Ryder Ryder Ryder. I don't understand books like this where it's okay for the main male character to be completely absurdly violent with everyone around them. He scares off everyone who even looks at Maddie, and then he looks at Maddie himself and scares her away from him. It's like UM who would ever go near the guy in the first place? And how is he not in jail?? He physically fights with random guys in bars, with Maddie's boyfriend, with his brother, with other random strangers, etc... etc... There absolutely IS such a thing as TOO MUCH VIOLENCE. He needs some serious anger management classes. <br><br>And he is the ULTIMATE cliche. Like c'mon seriously, tribal tattoos (um why? Is he in a tribe? Is this at all relevant to the story? Nope), complete womanizer, but in love with the best friend (in denial, of course), <b>obviously</b> like the best looking guy <i>ever</i>, typical cliche crap. Blah blah blah. Like, why is this even remotely attractive? If I met someone like him I'd run in the other direction. No thank you.<br><br>But seriously. The violence is out of control. I'll admit it starts to come in handy when the whole apocalypse thing happens, but considering how it was present way before that and then during it as well at times it didn't need to be.. UGH I don't understand why there are so many good reviews for this book. I NEVER get this passionate and write reviews like this, but this book just made me SO ANGRY. I HAD to get it all out so I could move on. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1385851909ra/7242491.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Will not be reading the sequel. I honestly couldn't care less if all of the characters died. Particularly Maddie, she kinda deserves it with all the dumb things she keeps doing. She brings danger to all of them and they'd be safer without her around. <br><br>0 stars</span>
  <a data-text-id="16222344018426994575" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_609450650" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/609450650" />
    <a title="Georgia ♥ " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/9138738-georgia"><img alt="Georgia ♥ " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1377186210p2/9138738.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/609450650?book_show_action=true">May 07, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Georgia ♥ " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Georgia ♥ " href="/user/show/9138738-georgia">Georgia ♥ </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/17788470-promise-me-darkness">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9138738-georgia?shelf=another-freaking-cliffhanger">another-freaking-cliffhanger</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9138738-georgia?shelf=tattoos-and-piercing">tattoos-and-piercing</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9138738-georgia?shelf=the-sound-of-my-heart-breaking">the-sound-of-my-heart-breaking</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9138738-georgia?shelf=apocalyptic-event">apocalyptic-event</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9138738-georgia?shelf=fantasy">fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9138738-georgia?shelf=2013">2013</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer609450650" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7797836400253572680"><b>3.5 I'm-Not-Really-Sure-What Stars<br/><br/><blockquote><i>"He was my darkness and I was his light.<br/>We couldn't exist without each other."</i></blockquote></b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380420703i/834848.jpg' width='400' height='299' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>Maddie & Ryder</b> two young kids, friends since childhood, deal with their feelings for each other, their shortcomings, war, heart break and the freaking Apocalypse, in this confusing but also strangely exciting novel by <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/7034900.Paige_Weaver' title='Paige Weaver' rel='nofollow noopener'>Paige Weaver</a>. Hard to put down, frustrating but in my opinion, a really good story that just has too much in its plate.<br/><br/><i>First and above all, this is a love story.</i><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380420703i/834849.jpg' width='325' height='325' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Maddie, a</span>
  <span id="freeText7797836400253572680" style="display:none"><b>3.5 I'm-Not-Really-Sure-What Stars<br><br><blockquote><i>"He was my darkness and I was his light.<br>We couldn't exist without each other."</i></blockquote></b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380420703i/834848.jpg" width="400" height="299" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Maddie &amp; Ryder</b> two young kids, friends since childhood, deal with their feelings for each other, their shortcomings, war, heart break and the freaking Apocalypse, in this confusing but also strangely exciting novel by <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/7034900.Paige_Weaver" title="Paige Weaver" rel="nofollow noopener">Paige Weaver</a>. Hard to put down, frustrating but in my opinion, a really good story that just has too much in its plate.<br><br><i>First and above all, this is a love story.</i><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380420703i/834849.jpg" width="325" height="325" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Maddie, a nursing student, has been in love with her childhood friend Ryder since forever. Despaired that he won't ever feel the same she is in another relationship and try to live her life. I liked her spark, sense of loyalty and sensibility. Sometimes it seems as though she suffers in silence and patiently waiting for Ryder to pull his head out of his ass for a minute and admit what is obvious from page 1. They belong together.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380402256ra/781740.gif" width="500" height="272" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Ryder is a stubborn, frustrating, hard-headed, love to hate male. Man whore, bad boy, tattooed and general bad ass, he feels inadequate of love and of Maddie. He think she deserves someone better than him. He can't help though, all the possessive and protective feelings he has toward her. He lives to take care of Maddie, but knowing he can't resist her for long, he decides to join the Army and even after sleeping together, he keeps pushing her away.<br><br><i>
  <b>“I fuck up all the time, Maddie. I don’t want to drag you down with me.” </b>
</i><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/536817.gif" width="400" height="220" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Stupid decision upon stupid decision, he keeps screwing up and regretting it. Running hot and cold, I think his insecurities really got old after a while and I just want to slap the shit out of him...<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380382446ra/740295.gif" width="400" height="280" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380401284ra/778697.gif" width="310" height="187" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>And this where the story, went post apocalyptic on us...</i><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380420703ra/834850.gif" width="400" height="220" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>This is also the point, where the story lost me and picked my interest at the same time. Somewhere in the middle, it turned out more. Terrorists attacked USA and all the power went off. It's the survival of the fittest and this when the book became a cross between the TV series, <i>Revolution</i> and <i>The Hunger Games</i>. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380420703i/834851._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="220" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Along with another couple, Maddie and Ryder must make a long journey to travel back home and to a possible sanctuary; fighting criminals, nature, themselves and each other in the way. Dealing with feelings, stubbornness, heartbreak and above all love, the trickiest feeling of all...<br><br><i>
  <b>"You see me for who I am, Maddie. Not my ghosts. Not my bad habits. Not my past. Just me. You’ve always seen just me.”</b>
</i><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380420703i/834852.gif" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Overall, this a book I enjoyed but can't say I loved. But it was a really great effort and I'm certainly intrigued enough to read the second. Maddie deserves a happily ever after and Ryder... well Ryder has to pull his shit together! <br><br><i>
  <b>“After sleeping with you, I vowed not to touch you again but when I thought I lost you tonight…my world collapsed,” he said, his voice husky. “All I wanted was to be able to kiss you one more time. And I did but I’m greedy. I want more.”</b>
</i><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380420703ra/834853.gif" width="400" height="180" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br></span>

<div id="review_644672993" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/644672993" />
    <a title="Anna" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/6744426-anna"><img alt="Anna" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1442117297p2/6744426.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/644672993?book_show_action=true">Jun 18, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Anna" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Anna" href="/user/show/6744426-anna">Anna</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>


          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">dystopia lovers</span></div>

        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer644672993" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12681138949758299370"><b> 4 LOVE-REMAINS-THE-SAME STARS !! </b><br/><br/><b>~ He was my darkness and I was his light. We couldn't exist without each other<br/> <br/>Ryder Delaney was the one imperfection in my life. He was the bad boy, the black sheep, the one your mother always warned you about. He had only one hard-and-fast rule - Don't fall in love~</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380425856i/850239._SY540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Lyrics by Gavin Rossdale •Love Remains the Same•❤<br/><br/><i>A thousand times I’ve seen you standing<br/>Gravity like a lunar landing<br/>Make me want to run till I find you<br/>I shut the world away from here<br/>Drift to you, yo</i></span>
  <span id="freeText12681138949758299370" style="display:none"><b> 4 LOVE-REMAINS-THE-SAME STARS !! </b><br><br><b>~ He was my darkness and I was his light. We couldn't exist without each other<br> <br>Ryder Delaney was the one imperfection in my life. He was the bad boy, the black sheep, the one your mother always warned you about. He had only one hard-and-fast rule - Don't fall in love~</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380425856i/850239._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Lyrics by Gavin Rossdale •Love Remains the Same•❤<br><br><i>A thousand times I’ve seen you standing<br>Gravity like a lunar landing<br>Make me want to run till I find you<br>I shut the world away from here<br>Drift to you, you’re all I hear<br><b>Everything we know fades to black<br><br>Half the time the world is ending<br>Truth is I am done pretending</b><br><br>I never thought that I had anymore to give<br>Pushing me so far<br>Here I am without you<br>Drink to all that we have lost<br>Mistakes we have made<br><b>Everything will change<br>But love remains the same</b></i><br><br><b>MADDIE</b><br><span>[image error]</span><br><br><b>RYDER</b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380425856i/850241.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><b>But sometimes Fate has a way of intervening. Soon our world collapsed. War erupted. Darkness prevailed. Alone and on the run, our only goal was to survive and to ignore the feelings we had for each other. But love is powerful...and so is the darkness</b><br><br>OKKKKKKKK......once again I found myself reading outside my normal box....this book fulfilled my challenge of reading a book of revolution/dystopia/apocalypse.....<b> well alrighty then here goes nuttin! </b><br><br>The first part of this book I was in <b>book butterfly heaven !!! my insides were gooey mush</b> It literally played out like a normal NA book. Ryder and Maddie were childhood best friends and next door neighbors in their remote Texas town. Maddie has always been in love with Ryder but he was placed firmly in her friend-zone because he was breathtaking and gorgeous and dangerous ~ All the ingredients for a typical man-whore. She watched him date girl after girl and spent many nights wishing it was her that he loved. She's 21 years old now, she's a virgin, she loves the bad boy leaving on a tour of duty.....*greedy me says BRING IT ON......<br><br><b> I'M ENLISTING IN THE ARMY .......but before I sign up, there is one thing that I want to do. </b>~ Ryder ....fess up something you want to do or SOMEONE you want to do ......come on now son!❤<br><br>So while I was off in lust-heaven.....all <b>HELL BROKE LOOSE !!!</b> just like that!<br><br>Next thing you know <b>...VISIONS OF ...THIS</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380425856i/850242._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Busted up my ❤ in-the-making-happily-ever-after <b>lots of visions of .....THIS</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380425856i/850243.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>and<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380425856i/850244.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>The remainder of the book was a story of<b> surviving.</b> Protecting whats yours. It was a combination of the Hunger Games and Divergent ( it was way steamyyyy though ) and some creep factors like in Revolution and the Walking Dead which is sooooooooooo not my thanggggg but I am forced to get ready for this "apocalypse" my husband and kids swear is gonna happen tomorrow. Will I read book 2 "Promise me Light" ? <b> HELL Yes, of course....I must know!! </b>. This is still a good love story and like with all love stories....I'm committed til the end of their happily-ever-after. <br><br>No matter what❤❤❤❤❤<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380425856i/850245.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I'm going to need this book right about now:<a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17862129.Promise_Me_Light__Promise_Me___2_" title="Promise Me Light (Promise Me, #2) by Paige Weaver" rel="nofollow noopener">

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer690434732" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8777474280475853330"><b> ✮ ✮ ✮ ✮ 5 HOT ALPHA MALE STARS ✮ ✮ ✮ ✮ </b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1381590524i/5073469._SY540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>
  <i>Promise Me Darkness,</i>
</b> was a super steamy, end of the world love story! I found it to be extremely unique in the sense that every other dystopian out there is focused more on the end of the world, and not the romance. The romance is the main focus of this story, of <b>Ryder & Maddie's</b> love for one another and the lengths they'll go to ensure each-others safety. <i>Promise Me Darkness</i> was filled with everything that I want in a romance:<b> love, alpha-male, jealou</b></span>
  <span id="freeText8777474280475853330" style="display:none"><b> ✮ ✮ ✮ ✮ 5 HOT ALPHA MALE STARS ✮ ✮ ✮ ✮ </b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1381590524i/5073469._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <i>Promise Me Darkness,</i>
</b> was a super steamy, end of the world love story! I found it to be extremely unique in the sense that every other dystopian out there is focused more on the end of the world, and not the romance. The romance is the main focus of this story, of <b>Ryder &amp; Maddie's</b> love for one another and the lengths they'll go to ensure each-others safety. <i>Promise Me Darkness</i> was filled with everything that I want in a romance:<b> love, alpha-male, jealous alpha male, possessive alpha male, tattooed alpha male...okay who am I kidding, Ryder stole the story!!</b><br><br>~.~.~.~.~.~.~.~.~.~.~.~.~.~.~.~.~.~.~.~.~.~.~.~.~.~.~.~.~.~.<br><br>Fate has a way of intervening. Soon their world collapsed. War erupted. Darkness prevailed. Alone and on the run, <b>Maddie and Ryder's</b> only goal was to survive and to ignore the feelings they have for each other. But their love is powerful...and so is the darkness that threatens to consume them...<br><br><b>Maddie</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1381594132i/5076850._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"You make me weak Maddie, so damn weak" ~Ryder</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br><b>Ryder</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1381594132i/5076851.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"Ryder Delaney was a legend. Women couldn't keep their hands off him and the men were scared to death of him. He was good looking and dangerous. A little bit bad and a whole lot sexy. ~Maddie </i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>Maddie and Ryder were childhood best friends and next door neighbors in the middle of nowhere Texas. Maddie is safe. She doesn't take risks or do daring things. She plays by the rules. That's why Ryder doesn't know she's in love with him...she's never had the courage to tell him. Not mention he's a total man whore who refuses to fall in love. Ryder might not have much of a choice to deny his feelings however, when foreign countries start attacking the United States, forcing Maddie and Ryder to stick together to survive. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1381593236i/5075993.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"What happened to we can't do this again?" he murmured against my mouth. I managed to get an answer out despite his hands slowly trailing up my my back. "It's just a kiss Ryder". "It's never just a kiss with you, Maddie. It's so much more."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>I loved loved loved this book! I can't wait to read the sequel. At first , I wasn't feeling it, but I stuck it out and it was so worth it! I love anything dystopian so this was right up my alley, not to mention <b>Ryder is a total alpha-male to the EXTREME.</b> I suggest anyone who loves a tattooed alpha male pick this one up!! <br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"You're all I need and want. Just you. Now and always." ~Ryder </i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br><br><b>
  <i>***I would recommend this novel to others***</i>
</b></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer4663963262030441048">This was honestly one of the best books I have read this year. I loved Ryder although at times his confusing behaviour was quite annoying he just kept giving conflicting messages that just wound me up a bit too. Maddie was sweet but sometimes her needy behaviour towards Ryder was just too much I understand about love and lust but just wish her character was a bit stronger and she wasn't so ruled by her physical reaction towards Ryder. I think the plot was great and the writing style really good.</span>
  <span id="freeText4663963262030441048" style="display:none">This was honestly one of the best books I have read this year. I loved Ryder although at times his confusing behaviour was quite annoying he just kept giving conflicting messages that just wound me up a bit too. Maddie was sweet but sometimes her needy behaviour towards Ryder was just too much I understand about love and lust but just wish her character was a bit stronger and she wasn't so ruled by her physical reaction towards Ryder. I think the plot was great and the writing style really good. I can't wait for the sequel hopefully we will get Ryders pov as I would love to understand his feelings about Maddie.</span>

  <span id="freeText14381839199453090973" style="display:none">Huh??<br><br><span>[image error]</span><br><br>Huh?<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/661471.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Hmm.....I'm not even sure what to say here. Ryder and Maddie have been BFFs since they were kids. Ryder has decided he is going to enlist in the Army and goes to stay with Maddie for a week. During this time, terrorist threats are high. <div id="review_596419773" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/596419773" />
    <a title="Wendy" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/10593171-wendy"><img alt="Wendy" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1367039241p2/10593171.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/596419773?book_show_action=true">Apr 21, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Wendy" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Wendy" href="/user/show/10593171-wendy">Wendy</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10593171-wendy?shelf=tops">tops</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer596419773" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16945128492836825174"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380418517i/828752.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Fuck me!!! When is the next book coming out?????? MUST.HAVE.MORE!<br/><br/>Okay, I took a day to read something for myself. I picked PROMISE ME DARKNESS by Author Paige Weaver. I really had no idea what to expect with this book, but:<br/>HOLYFUCKINGBADBOYBOOKBOYFRIENDSEXYMOTHERFUCKER!!!!<br/>I absolutely LOVE this book! ♥ ♥ ♥<br/>Please do not let the synopsis throw you. I went into this thinking it was going to be another sweet easy read about college love. FUCK NO!!! I was blindsided and smacked right upside the head.</span>
  <span id="freeText16945128492836825174" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380418517i/828752.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Fuck me!!! When is the next book coming out?????? MUST.HAVE.MORE!<br><br>Okay, I took a day to read something for myself. I picked PROMISE ME DARKNESS by Author Paige Weaver. I really had no idea what to expect with this book, but:<br>HOLYFUCKINGBADBOYBOOKBOYFRIENDSEXYMOTHERFUCKER!!!!<br>I absolutely LOVE this book! ♥ ♥ ♥<br>Please do not let the synopsis throw you. I went into this thinking it was going to be another sweet easy read about college love. FUCK NO!!! I was blindsided and smacked right upside the head. There is no easy about this, it really is a dark and kind of twisted story, but worth every damn page turning moment. <br><br>Maddie and Ryder have been best friends since early childhood having grown up as neighbors. <br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380418517i/828753.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Maddie has always been secretly in love with her best friend who also happens to be the biggest man-whore she knows. Ryder is finished with college and back home. Maddie is home for summer break before going back to nursing school. One night, Ryder gives Maddie some news and asks her if he can come stay with her and her roommate Eva for a few days when they go back to campus. <br>Talk about sexual tension!!! <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380418517i/828754.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> Yes!!! it's everywhere! <br><br>Maddie has a bad run in with her boyfriend, yes she has a boyfriend, Ben, and Ryder is there to play hero. Now Maddie is starting to feel confused. But really, when you read this book you'll understand why at times her confusion is warranted. <br><br>If I wasn't already such a huge fan of Ryder at this point, I may have wanted to bitch slap him. Okay, I still did at times want to, but I really wanted to knock some sense into both he and Maddie. <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380380128ra/736771.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>And then, CHAOS!!! <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380395440ra/761683.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Four 20 something's start a journey that should only take mere hours but turns into days. At this point in the book, I'm beyond freaking out. I've got heart palpitations, my gut is clenching and my eyes are starting to tear up from the most random occurrences. <br><br>After reaching their destination, heart ache ensues in two different forms for Maddie. The daily struggles in the "new world" are definitely a trial. <br><br>I can without a doubt say that this book is gritty, intense and full of sexual angst/tension and at times heartbreaking. The darkness surrounding this story is something that could very well happen and it eludes to that nerve wracking fear that would occur if it became a reality.<br>Right away I almost felt like I was in the show Revolution and I loved it! Please don't let that thought scare you, it's only based on how I felt the story line go, but it quickly changed and I was right along with Maddie on her journey.<br><br>My cast: <br><br>Ryder<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380418517i/828755.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Maddie<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380418517i/828756.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>
  <a data-text-id="16945128492836825174" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer587460861" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8672224954093293652">Wow, having not read the synopsis but diving straight in this book was not what I expected at all. I was fully prepared for a feel good best friends falling in love type book with the typical drama that ensues, but this was so much more. Sure, we have that storyline in the mix, but that is in admist a war that has broken out. Instead of a book about daisies and sunshine, you get a scarily real depiction of what would happen if a war broke out in america, and it was every man for himself. The thi</span>
  <span id="freeText8672224954093293652" style="display:none">Wow, having not read the synopsis but diving straight in this book was not what I expected at all. I was fully prepared for a feel good best friends falling in love type book with the typical drama that ensues, but this was so much more. Sure, we have that storyline in the mix, but that is in admist a war that has broken out. Instead of a book about daisies and sunshine, you get a scarily real depiction of what would happen if a war broke out in america, and it was every man for himself. The things people do to survive... this book gives you a haunting look into the lives of these four teenagers who have to face unimaginable hurdles through the texan sun to make it to safety. And even when you think everything will be okay, you realise the war has not ended this book is just the beginning!<br /><br />I CAN NOT WAIT for the next book. With that epic cliffhanger ending, I need to know what happens! Great book, definitely recommend it to those who love romance, war and survival books! <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ thank god he finally admitted his feelings, i was about to pull my hair out in frustration from the back and forth these two had going on  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br /> </span>

  <span id="freeText12470157517696102756" style="display:none">So I don't know what book all of the negative reviewers read but it couldn't have been this one. This story was actually refreshing not like all the others that are all high power male/ female sex driven story lines. <br />Scary part is that the theory in this story is probably true. I'm seriously thinking that I may want to stock more canned goods in the house. <br />But back to the story...Maddie yes was somewhat of a pushover and a prisoner to her love for Ryder but she had her strengths and didn't give up even in her two significant life threatening situations in the book. Ryder was super protective with a fierceness you didn't want to even test. Yes for whatever reason his lack of wanting to state his obvious love for Maddie was a bit frustrating, but it wouldn't be a story if he gave into easily now would it be. I am a bit annoyed that Eva &amp; Brody separated from them, but again then where would the second book go....I loved Eva by the way, Maddie &amp; her friendship was endearing and I hope all works out in the second book. So when will it be coming out??????</span>

<div id="review_740954417" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/740954417" />
    <a title="AJ" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3143126-aj"><img alt="AJ" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1406382884p2/3143126.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/740954417?book_show_action=true">Oct 13, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="AJ" class="user" itemprop="url" name="AJ" href="/user/show/3143126-aj">AJ</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=romantic">romantic</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=duet">duet</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=post-apocalyptic">post-apocalyptic</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer740954417" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17226944218470511560">This book was definitely not what I was expecting. I was expecting a swoony romance set against a post-apocalyptic warzone. Not quite! Instead we get an angsty romance which just happens to take place following an attack on the US which leaves everybody without power, and a few desperate people running around… occasionally. That may sound really negative, but I definitely don’t intend it to be, because although parts of this book are very familiar, the setting, and the challenges faced by the ch</span>
  <span id="freeText17226944218470511560" style="display:none">This book was definitely not what I was expecting. I was expecting a swoony romance set against a post-apocalyptic warzone. Not quite! Instead we get an angsty romance which just happens to take place following an attack on the US which leaves everybody without power, and a few desperate people running around… occasionally. That may sound really negative, but I definitely don’t intend it to be, because although parts of this book are very familiar, the setting, and the challenges faced by the characters are actually really original. <br /><br />It’s the story of Maddie, an innocent, somewhat naïve girl who is in love with her neighbour and childhood best friend, Ryder, who just happens to be a smoking hot, tattooed, manwhoring bad boy. Stop me if you’ve heard this one before. Oh, and did I forget to mention – she’s a virgin! Ding, ding, ding! All necessary NA boxes ticked.<br /><br />But unlike other books with a similar set up, just when things start to get interesting between Maddie and Ryder, the US is attacked by terrorists, sparking what could be WWIII, and throwing the entire country into turmoil. Desperate to get home to their families, and with Maddie injured following a nightclub stampede, they set off with Maddie’s best friend Eva, and her boyfriend Brody to travel to their home town, along the way having to search for food, water and shelter in the sweltering heat of summer, and deal with violent bad guys, all while wading through the angst of their maybe/maybe not relationship.<br /><br />And about that relationship... Holy effing hell. So. Freaking. Frustrating! And I feel the need to rant, so here it comes…<br /><br />Obviously Maddie and Ryder are hot for each other, and there is a bit of hotness that goes on, which is very nice, but it all starts to go to hell when Ryder throws Maddie what is possibly the biggest cop-out in romance:<br /><br /><i>“I know you want it all. Love, a relationship. But I can’t give that to you. I won’t because I’ll just end up hurting you.”</i><br /><br />Ugh! Seriously? And if that’s not enough, the boy throws off mixed messages like nothing else! One minute he’s all caring, protective, and alpha over her, and the next he’s pissed off and completely ignoring her. God, I wanted to punch him so hard! <br /><br />And it’s not a one time thing, he’s up and down for the entire book. But it’s not just him. If Maddie stopped being such a sap and instead of wasting her time whining about how she’s only going to be friends with Ryder and actually confronted him, maybe she would have got some answers. It’s one of those books where you just want to grab the two main characters, smack their heads together and scream at them to TALK TO EACH OTHER, AND SORT YOUR SHIT OUT!!! But instead, Maddie (amidst her own TSTL moments that prove she is also in need of a punch) just stands by while Ryder is an ass and constantly pushes her away. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[And she actually lives with him! Loving him so much, that she needs to be with him even though he’s ignoring her while she just sits there and waits for him like a good little doormat. And then… when he finally comes to his senses, he spouts this at her…<br /><br /><i>“I’ve missed you … God, I’ve missed you so much.”<br />…<br />“I can’t get enough of you … I’ve been in misery without you.”</i><br /><br />All very heartfelt, but it just made me want to scream at him – IT’S YOUR OWN STUPID FAULT, ASSHOLE! <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br />OK, rant over. And after all of that, I must confess that while I was supremely annoyed at his behaviour, I really <i>want</i> to love Ryder, and I do actually like him. He manages to balance just enough sweetness and what is obviously deep love for Maddie to have me clutching my heart, before he goes and says something that makes him a total douche. <br /><br />Although, I am happy to report that he does get his act together, and in a very late reprieve, finally gets in touch with his feelings, and THEN we get the swoon.<br /><br /><i>“You’re all I need and want. Just you. Now and always.”<br />… <br />“I’m yours, Maddie and I’ll love you for the rest of my life”</i><br /><br />Awwwww<a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www">www</a>... just in time to win my heart!<br /><br />Despite all of the angst, and my constant eye rolling, there is something about this book that sucked me in. I care about these characters, I want them be together, I was interested the entire way through the book, and I’m desperate to find out what happens next in the story. There are some very intriguing story threads to be played out, plus the threat of the war getting closer to them. I’m excited for the big conclusion.<br /><br />3.5 frustrating, but full of potential for a big ending, stars.<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="17226944218470511560" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_631988216" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/631988216" />
    <a title="axola" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/9835698-axola"><img alt="axola" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1408998923p2/9835698.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/631988216?book_show_action=true">Jun 03, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="axola" class="user" itemprop="url" name="axola" href="/user/show/9835698-axola">axola</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer631988216" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1100745737281540177"><b> 75% into this book, I decided the only reasonable thing to do was quit it before I ended up punching my computer. The plot was ruined by the most annoying characters ever. You know, the kind of characters you imagine killing every chapter.</b><br/>The idea was actually a good one. I think is only the second book I've read with a similar plot (which nowadays is nearly a miracle). However, the stupidity of the characters ruined it for me (and that before knowing there was going to be a second book).<br/><br/>The pl</span>
  <span id="freeText1100745737281540177" style="display:none"><b> 75% into this book, I decided the only reasonable thing to do was quit it before I ended up punching my computer. The plot was ruined by the most annoying characters ever. You know, the kind of characters you imagine killing every chapter.</b><br />The idea was actually a good one. I think is only the second book I've read with a similar plot (which nowadays is nearly a miracle). However, the stupidity of the characters ruined it for me (and that before knowing there was going to be a second book).<br /><br />The plot is quite straightforward: 4 friends find themselves needing to get home from the university after USA has suffered an attack which has put down, electricity, communications... (Does NBC's Revolution ring a bell?).<br /><br />The problem is that we spend the first 70% of this book nearly alone with 4 characters that would drive any sane person to death. Let's start with our hero and heroine:<br /><br /><b> Maddie, our heroine is our usual new adult book stereotype heroine. You know, 21, VIRGIN, supposedly clever (several new adult books definitely have me thinking that intelligence is not a requirement to get into university anymore) and IN LOVE WITH A MANWHORE. <br />Maddie is sometimes a pushover, sometimes stubborn, but 100% of the times she is just plain STUPID. </b><br /><br /><u> First we have her relationship with Ryder</u>. Friends since kids, she acts deeply surprised and offended because after sleeping with her Ryder says he doesn't want something serious with her. WTF is she surprised or annoyed by that? She knows this guy, she slept with him when it was pretty clear by his actions and comments he wasn't thinking about happily ever after. So girl give us a rest! <br />But even worse was that afterwards we have to listen to her inner dialogue constantly going something like this: " Wow, Ryder is so sexy and every time we get close (or humping each other) I get so hot, but No, NO! He doesn't love me, so we can't have anything...oohhh, but he gets me so hot every time he looks at me....ohhhh...." This goes forever!!!!!<br /><br />Secondly, <u> this girl is too stupid to live </u>. She goes into a fit because after 2 days of walking on the road (by her and her whinny friend's fault btw), they decide to break and enter into an abandoned house. For F*cks shake the house is abandoned, you have no food, no water and still we have to hear you complaining? With a broken rib and hand they tell you to hide yourself because there could be danger, but hell no...no way you are doing that because even though your presence could be potentially dangerous if taken as hostage you are not going to let anyone put you aside? ... Just 2 examples, but trust me I could write and write with more example.<br /><br /><b> Hunter is the 24 ass#ole- manw#ore that sometimes acts like a psychopath and sometimes like Maddie's puppy. </b> If there was a time to be a controlling ass#ole is when you have to try and get home 3 of the most dumb people ever...But noooooo....we get the psychopath every time someone looks at Maddie and the puppy every time she puts herself and everyone else in danger. <br /><br /><b> Eva, the friend from hell </b>. If you are still reading this overly large review, after reading my description of Maddie you can imagine what to expect of her best friend. Yeah...another too stupid to live person, who can even decide from one chapter to the other whether Maddie should hook up with Ryder. Even worse by that is the scene where they lost the car they were driving because the stupid girl decides to play Mother Theresa in what is obviously a trap! But even worse is that about a chapter later, she gets mad for hiding instead of asking a ride from 4 drunk men. Can you be more stupid? Wtf do you think is going to happen if you stop that car? I don't know...but being robbed and molested a chapter before, you could maybe imagine it! Call me crazy!!<br /><br />This has gone too long so I won't even bother you talking about the 4th member of the expedition. Because, really do you really need to know more? <br /><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="1100745737281540177" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_957795605" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/957795605" />
    <a title="Leslie" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5433591-leslie"><img alt="Leslie" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1583458638p2/5433591.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/957795605?book_show_action=true">Jun 04, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Leslie" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Leslie" href="/user/show/5433591-leslie">Leslie</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5433591-leslie?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5433591-leslie?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5433591-leslie?shelf=steamy">steamy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5433591-leslie?shelf=alpha-male">alpha-male</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5433591-leslie?shelf=sexy">sexy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5433591-leslie?shelf=great-writing">great-writing</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer957795605" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2026594902758875671">What happens when you pick up a book almost completely blind of it's premise but only know the genre? Well, let me tell ya, you get a huge smile on your face from utter delight because, uh, huh...it was THAT great! <br/><br/>I'm a sucker for good writing, first and foremost. If a story is in anyway cliche' or the same ole, same ole of "insta-love" and/or "insta-lust", with regurgitated phrases like: "He was the most beautiful man I had ever seen" or "He smelled of leather and musk", I'm out before the sec</span>
  <span id="freeText2026594902758875671" style="display:none">What happens when you pick up a book almost completely blind of it's premise but only know the genre? Well, let me tell ya, you get a huge smile on your face from utter delight because, uh, huh...it was THAT great! <br /><br />I'm a sucker for good writing, first and foremost. If a story is in anyway cliche' or the same ole, same ole of "insta-love" and/or "insta-lust", with regurgitated phrases like: "He was the most beautiful man I had ever seen" or "He smelled of leather and musk", I'm out before the second chapter begins. Not to mention, having to seriously rest my overly rolled eye balls. Oh, but that's so not the case with this novel. (Thank God.) The incredibly easy flow and descriptive way Weaver tells her dystopian romance with cleverness and wit, along with a swoon-worthy alpha-male named, "Ryder"...I mean, seriously, I was a goner.<br /><br />Let's face it y'all, there's been an explosion of new indie authors uploading to Amazon on a minute by minute basis. Only trouble is, the market is so over saturated with so many choices, it's beyond the proverbial "needle in a haystack" to find the really good ones. And that's where I come in, because reviews are just about the only way a reader can gage what's worth their sacred "one-click" anymore. Now, I must state the fact that Ms. Weaver certainly doesn't need my praise or my pimping because she's already experienced huge success with all her books. I'm merely the total idiot who, until now, completely missed the freaking boat. *face palm*<br /><br />I will warn you, there is a cliffhanger at the end and if I'm being completely honest, I'm not the biggest fan of those - but if this tells you anything, I SIMPLY DON'T CARE! I'm happy and pretty darn excited to one-cllick the next installment (Promise Me Light) just as soon as I hit save. <br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="2026594902758875671" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_598504184" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/598504184" />
    <a title="Jules" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/7297440-jules"><img alt="Jules" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1336592154p2/7297440.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/598504184?book_show_action=true">Apr 23, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jules" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jules" href="/user/show/7297440-jules">Jules</a>
      </span>

          added it




        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7297440-jules?shelf=dnf">dnf</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7297440-jules?shelf=too-juvenile-to-be-enjoyable">too-juvenile-to-be-enjoyable</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7297440-jules?shelf=nonsensical-characterization">nonsensical-characterization</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7297440-jules?shelf=innocent-really">innocent-really</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
                  <em>
                    This review has been hidden because it contains spoilers. To view it,
                    <a href="#" onclick="Effect.toggle(&#39;reviewTextContainer598504184&#39;); return false;">click here.</a>
                  </em>
              <span id="reviewTextContainer598504184" class="readable"
                    style="display:none"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5302753960104902277">Marked as DNF. no rating<br/>I couldn't finish this book for several reasons. I tried to give it the benefit of the doubt. I entertained thoughts of,<i>slow start, it will warm up, right?</i> Wrong.<br/>Things that don't make sense:<br/>I want Maddie to have at least some backbone. If you don't want to drink whiskey from a dirty glass, say no and stick to it. Don't ponder how disgusting it is and then drink both shots while chalking it up to a sacrifice for a friend. Nonsense.<br/>Eve and Maddie go to a bar with scary tat</span>
  <span id="freeText5302753960104902277" style="display:none">Marked as DNF. no rating<br />I couldn't finish this book for several reasons. I tried to give it the benefit of the doubt. I entertained thoughts of,<i>slow start, it will warm up, right?</i> Wrong.<br />Things that don't make sense:<br />I want Maddie to have at least some backbone. If you don't want to drink whiskey from a dirty glass, say no and stick to it. Don't ponder how disgusting it is and then drink both shots while chalking it up to a sacrifice for a friend. Nonsense.<br />Eve and Maddie go to a bar with scary tattooed men. These two girls are types: the innocent and the hell-raiser. I understand the hell-raiser type in Eva that she wants to dance, drink, and live it up. What I don't understand is why she and Maddie spend even 2 minutes together as friends. The relationship is grounded in annoyance. It doesn't make sense.<br />I wanted Eva to be cool, knowledgeable, hip and urbane. She wasn't. She states the obvious and punctuates everything with shouting:<br /><br />“TABLE!" Eva squealed when she saw two empty chairs. Pulling on my hand, she charged forward, bumping into a couple of leather– clad men who scowled at us. At least the seats were in the corner. Maybe no one will notice us here. Eva could have her fun and then we could leave. Hopefully, in one piece. "WOOO HOOO!” Eva shrieked as one of her favorite rap songs started blasting from the speakers. It earned us a few more dirty looks.<br /><br />I want Maddie to be as intelligent as suggested by her nursing career. I find it ridiculous that both girls are college-smart, but lack common sense. They behave provocatively in a bar Maddie decides is scary and dangerous:<br /><br />"By the second song, we were having a good time. Eva turned to shake her butt at me, sending me into fits of laughter. We started rubbing against each other, grinding to the music and acting silly. After the song ended, I noticed we had gathered an audience. Many of the rough looking men were now standing on the sidelines, watching us. I nervously scanned the crowd, afraid we were over our heads."<br /><br />Maybe I'm just too old and conservative to find bumping and grinding with a girlfriend on the dance floor to be a random accident. Oops! We didn't know we were creating a lascivious feast for the eyes when we simulated girl-on-girl sex on the dance floor - whoopsie!<br /><br />At this point, I find both of them annoying. Make it stop!<br /><br />The male lead is not swoon-worthy. I found little evidence as to why Maddie is hung up on him other than proximity. He is there. He has been there forever. Where are the interesting anecdotes about how caring his is? Yeah, not there. Too much telling and no showing.<br />The first time we see Ryder, he's in a fight with a man much bigger than he is, but he manages to take the huge guy down. I'd much prefer a hero who admits he's smaller, uses the element of surprise, and then exits swiftly. That makes more sense than having him inexplicably destroy someone much larger. In addition Ryder is a jerk and doesn't make sense. He loves Maddie to death. He will fight for her. He wants to have sex with her. He regrets having sex with her. The sex is meaningless. <br /><br />I'm just so done with books that have idiot protagonists, energizer bunny best friends, and abusive asshole boyfriends for the sake of a little angst later.</span>
  <a data-text-id="5302753960104902277" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<span id="freeTextContainer1157468975172071101">You knows those books that suck you in from the beginning? The ones that you just cannot put down? Well, Promise me Darkness was one of those books for me. <br/><br/>Maddie is a 21 year old nurse student who's been best friends with bad boy Ryder for 15 years, despite their different ways of life. Maddie is the complete opposite of Ryder, the typical good girl, goes to school and studies, doesn't drink or smoke and stays out of trouble and only dates gentlemen. But with everything in her life going to the</span>
  <span id="freeText1157468975172071101" style="display:none">You knows those books that suck you in from the beginning? The ones that you just cannot put down? Well, Promise me Darkness was one of those books for me. <br /><br />Maddie is a 21 year old nurse student who's been best friends with bad boy Ryder for 15 years, despite their different ways of life. Maddie is the complete opposite of Ryder, the typical good girl, goes to school and studies, doesn't drink or smoke and stays out of trouble and only dates gentlemen. But with everything in her life going to the way she wants it too there is still one thing Maddie wants but can't have, and that's Ryder. <br />Ryder, well, he's a legend. The women can't keeps there hands off him and the men are scored to death of him. Ryder has one rule. Don't fall in love. <br /><br /><br />Was this a romance? Yes, definitely. But this book was so much more.. Love, friendships, family and i felt all of these emotions along with struggle and survival when the unthinkable happens.<br /><br /><br />I thoroughly enjoyed this book, it was a fantastic, beautiful and emotional read and I am very much looking forward to read the sequel 'Promise me Light'<br /><br />X</span>

<span id="freeTextContainer14870179045319016321">I absolutely loved this book. I figured it was gonna be your average childhood love story. Girl goes off to college & then the stubborn sexy guy from her childhood finally comes to his senses. But NO!! That's not at all what happens. This book surprised me & took a totally different turn that I never saw coming. The direction the author took was so refreshing. Yes, of course you still have the gorgeous, tattooed, stubborn, sexy guy. Wouldn't be a great book without him. At times I would get so f</span>
  <span id="freeText14870179045319016321" style="display:none">I absolutely loved this book. I figured it was gonna be your average childhood love story. Girl goes off to college &amp; then the stubborn sexy guy from her childhood finally comes to his senses. But NO!! That's not at all what happens. This book surprised me &amp; took a totally different turn that I never saw coming. The direction the author took was so refreshing. Yes, of course you still have the gorgeous, tattooed, stubborn, sexy guy. Wouldn't be a great book without him. At times I would get so frustrated with him but just like Maddie, I loved him so much! So many other people who reviewed this book complained that Maddie wasn't strong enough &amp; I guess was lacking that "girl power". But I disagree. Several times in this book she fought hard. She even fought with the the one guys she loves. I loved everything about this book. There is a cliffhanger in the end but not a huge one that leaves you very ticked off when the book ends. It's just enough to really tease you &amp; wanting so badly to read the next book. Can't wait!! :)</span>

  <span id="freeText10670042072980457079" style="display:none">I am left speechless over this book , I am literally at a loss searching my mind for just the rights words to express how well written this book is . This book needs to be a movie hands down it is that good. After reading this I felt like crocodile dundee when he said "that's not a knife , this is a knife !" This suspense and drama with what will happen next betweem Ryder and Maddie in the middle of all this terror - And it makes you think , really think what if something like this were to take place on American soil that only made me relate to them so much more because in thinking that and how we all are really so dependent on electricity and electronic forms of communication it is beyond terrifying - This is a must read ! And the price is a steal at only $0.99 are you kidding !! I have bought and paid good money for books and felt robbed very few make me feel as if I stole from the authour , this one is being sold far below it's value - Can't wait for the next book !!! </span>
